[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJNI global refs: [0m[1;36m26[0m[39m, weak refs: [0m[1;36m0[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libFuzzer run against the `CompressTarFuzzer` harness reported a timeout after [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapproximately [0m[1;36m27[0m[39m seconds. The main thread was found stuck in Java’s big-integer [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdivision routines [0m[1;39m([0m[39mspecifically `MutableBigInteger.divideOneWord` and related [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethods[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m while parsing PAX header timestamps in the Apache Commons Compress TAR [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation. No crash or exception was raised—execution simply exceeded the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer’s time limit.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- What the issue is  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The fuzzer timed out while executing `CompressTarFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`. The [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJava thread dump shows the main thread in a deep call stack centered on [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`java.math.MutableBigInteger.divideOneWord` and associated division routines, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39multimately invoked by `TarArchiveEntry.parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds`. This [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicates that parsing of decimal-encoded timestamps in PAX headers can drive the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBigDecimal/BigInteger division logic into a long-running state.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Although not explicitly labeled in the report, this behavior aligns with a [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresource-exhaustion or performance vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpotential Denial-of-Service[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhere specially crafted input causes excessive computation and leads to timeouts.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations and findings  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The stall originates in `BigInteger.divideKnuth` and [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`BigDecimal.divideAndRound` as called by [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`BigDecimal.createAndStripZerosToMatchScale`.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `TarArchiveEntry.parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds` invokes these BigDecimal [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroutines to process timestamp values extracted from PAX headers.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer entry point [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`CompressTarFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m simply [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstructs a `TarFile` on the provided byte array, triggering full PAX-header [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • No native or application-specific code is shown to fault; the expensive [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation is purely in standard Java math and the Commons Compress library.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas for investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To gain a holistic view, inspect:  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.tar.TarArchiveEntry.parseInstantFromDecimalS[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meconds` and its handling of decimal strings.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • PAX-header processing in `TarArchiveEntry.processPaxHeader` and [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TarFile.applyPaxHeadersToCurrentEntry` [0m[35m/[0m[39m `TarFile.paxHeaders`.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • BigDecimal creation and scaling logic in [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`java.math.BigDecimal.createAndStripZerosToMatchScale`, `divideAndRound`, and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrelated `BigInteger` division methods.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzz harness `CompressTarFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` as the entry point for [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggering this behavior.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat replaces the expensive BigDecimal operations with manual string parsing of the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseconds and fractional parts. After applying the patch, the build failed with a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompilation error: `cannot find symbol method [0m[1;35mrepeat[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in the manual parsing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial Issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- During fuzz testing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia Jazzer/libFuzzer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the `CompressTarFuzzer` hung and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meventually timed out.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The thread dump shows the fuzzer thread stuck deep in [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`java.math.MutableBigInteger.divideOneWord` and related BigDecimal division methods[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalled from `TarArchiveEntry.parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds`.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The symptom is a prolonged CPU burn in BigDecimal quotient/remainder logic, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleading to a detected “timeout” by libFuzzer.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Other JVM threads are idle or performing unrelated GC and housekeeping tasks; the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmain thread is RUNNABLE and cycling in BigInteger/BigDecimal code.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In `TarArchiveEntry.java`, the BigDecimal-based parsing  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```java[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  final BigDecimal epochSeconds = new [0m[1;35mBigDecimal[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvalue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  final long seconds = [0m[1;35mepochSeconds.longValue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  final long nanos = [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mepochSeconds.remainder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mBigDecimal.ONE[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.movePointRight[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m9[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.longValue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  was replaced with manual string splitting:  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Determine sign and split at the decimal point  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Parse seconds with `[0m[1;35mLong.parseLong[0m[1;39m([0m[39msecondsPart[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Normalize and pad the fraction part to [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m digits, then parse with [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mLong.parseLong[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfrac[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Apply the sign to nanoseconds if needed  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Call `[0m[1;35mInstant.ofEpochSecond[0m[1;39m([0m[39mseconds, nanos[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The new code uses `[0m[1;35mString.repeat[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to pad zeros in the fraction portion.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Result  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The Maven build recompiled the changed sources but failed at compile time:  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  `[0m[35m/src/.../[0m[95mTarArchiveEntry.java[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m290[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m34[0m[1;39m][0m[39m cannot find symbol method [0m[1;35mrepeat[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This indicates that `[0m[1;35mString.repeat[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is not available under the configured [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJava source/target level [0m[1;39m([0m[39mJava [0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, leading to a build failure.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAreas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Verify the configured Java source and target versions in the Maven compiler [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mplugin and adjust language features accordingly.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Review the `parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds` method in `TarArchiveEntry` for [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompatibility with Java [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor the project’s minimum supported Java[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Examine any utility methods or libraries used for zero-padding rather than [0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Check the PAX header parsing logic for edge cases [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvery large integers, negative [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Replace the Java [0m[1;36m11[0m[39m+ `[0m[1;35mString.repeat[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call in [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds` with a Java [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m–compatible padding mechanism [0m[1;39m([0m[39musing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.lang3.StringUtils`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and reapply the manual-split approach for [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhigh performance.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Detailed Steps[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Add Import[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - At the top of `TarArchiveEntry.java`, alongside existing imports, add:[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        import org.apache.commons.lang3.StringUtils;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This pulls in the Commons-Lang3 utility for string padding [0m[1;39m([0m[39malready on the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclasspath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Replace `String.repeat` with `StringUtils.rightPad`[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In the `parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds` method, remove the `frac = frac + [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"0"[0m[1;35m.repeat[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - After computing `fractionPart`, write:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Truncate or pad the fraction to exactly [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m digits[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        String frac = [0m[1;35mfractionPart.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > [0m[1;36m9[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            ? [0m[1;35mfractionPart.substring[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m9[0m[1;39m)[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            : [0m[1;35mStringUtils.rightPad[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfractionPart, [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m, [0m[32m'0'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Then parse `nanos` from `frac` as before and apply the `negative` sign if [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mneeded.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Preserve Validation and Error Handling[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Keep the existing regex check [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`PAX_EXTENDED_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_FILE_TIMES_PATTERN`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand exception messages to ensure malformed inputs still throw `IOException`.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Retain the final `[0m[1;35mInstant.ofEpochSecond[0m[1;39m([0m[39mseconds, nanos[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` wrapped in a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtry-catch for `DateTimeException` and `ArithmeticException`.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Why This Works[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mStringUtils.rightPad[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr, [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m, [0m[32m'0'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` pads or truncates to a fixed width in Java[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m.[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No reliance on BigDecimal arithmetic, eliminating the fuzzer timeout root [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maintains identical behavior for:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Inputs without a decimal point [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfraction treated as `[0m[1;36m000000000[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Inputs with fewer than [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m fractional digits [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpadded[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Inputs with more than [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m digits [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtruncated[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Negative values [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfraction sign inverted[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Trailing decimal points [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[32m"123."[0m[39m` yields fractionPart `[0m[32m""[0m[39m` → `[0m[32m"000000000"[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Side-Effect Mitigation[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Commons-Lang3 is already a dependency [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `SystemProperties` import[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdding `StringUtils` does not introduce new external libraries.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness or test code is modified; all existing tests and fuzz targets [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinue to operate unchanged.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure imports are organized to avoid unused warnings.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Patch Context Reference[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - File: [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/tar/TarArchiveEntry.java`[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Method: `private static Instant [0m[1;35mparseInstantFromDecimalSeconds[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString value[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This patch restores Java [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m compatibility, preserves the manual string‐parsing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperformance optimization that avoids BigDecimal, and ensures the code compiles [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munder the existing Maven compiler settings without resorting to unsupported Java [0m[1;36m11[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAPIs.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
